			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = ARM_democration_opposition_1
					}
				}
				add_ideas = ARM_democration_opposition_1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ARM_democration_opposition_1
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ARM_democration_opposition_1
					add_idea = ARM_democration_opposition_2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ARM_democration_opposition_2
				}
				add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^4 = 0.05 }
				recalculate_party = yes
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
		}
